if (!theForm) {

    theForm = document.aspnetForm;

function __doPostBack(eventTarget, eventArgument) {

    if (!theForm.onsubmit || (theForm.onsubmit() != false)) {

        theForm.__EVENTTARGET.value = eventTarget;

        theForm.__EVENTARGUMENT.value = eventArgument;

        theForm.submit();

    }

}

       <script type="text/javascript">

 

 

        var CurrentUser = null;

        function getUser() {

 



            $('#txtUserName').val('');

            $('#txtPassword').val('');

            CurrentUser = null;

            try {

 



                ExecuteOrDelayUntilScriptLoaded(function () {

 



                    var context = new SP.ClientContext.get_current();

                    var web = context.get_web();

                    var currentUser = web.get_currentUser();

                    currentUser.retrieve();

                    context.load(web);

                    context.executeQueryAsync(function () {

 

                        var userObject = web.get_currentUser();

 

                        try {

                            var email = userObject.get_email();

                            var id = userObject.get_id();

                            var loginName = userObject.get_loginName();

                            var title = userObject.get_title();

                            CurrentUser = title;

                            $('#txtUserName').val(title);

                            $('#txtPassword').val(title);

                            console.log(userObject);

                            setUser();

 

                        }

                        catch (err) {

 

                            console.log(err);

                            CurrentUser = null;

                            $('#txtUserName').val('');

                            $('#txtPassword').val('');

                            setUser();

                        }

                    }, function (o, args) {

 

                        return callback(args.get_message());

                    });

                }, "sp.js");

 

            }

            catch (err) {

                CurrentUser = null;

                console.log(err);

                $('#txtUserName').val('');

                $('#txtPassword').val('');

                setUser();

            }

        }

 

 

        function setUser() {

 

            if (CurrentUser == null) {

 



                $('#group-usuarios').hide();

                $('#group-broadcast').hide();

                //crearChatUsuario({ Origen: { GUID: '2', PrimerNombre: 'Sala Dos',Mensaje:'' } });

                //crearChatUsuario({ Origen: { GUID: '3', PrimerNombre: 'Sala Tres', Mensaje: '' } });

                $('#labelUser').text('Correo');

                $('#labelPassword').text('Nombre');

 

            }

            else {

                $('#group-salas').hide();

 

            }

        }

 

        var dialog;

        $(document).ready(function () {

 



            //dialog = $("#dialog").dialog();

 

            getUser();

 

 



        });

         debugger;

            window.open('/Style%20Library/ACChat/modalchat.html?Id=' + $('#txtUserName').val(), "_blank", "width=1200,height=700,scrollbars=no,menubar=false,status=no,titlebar=no,toolbar=false,reziseable=yes");

        }

function _RegisterWebPartPageCUI()

{

    var initInfo = {editable: false,isEditMode: false,allowWebPartAdder: false,listId: "{55d84f57-c2d0-447d-8ace-0655b9927ab9}",itemId: 2,recycleBinEnabled: true,enableMinorVersioning: true,enableModeration: false,forceCheckout: true,rootFolderUrl: "\u002fPages",itemPermissions:{High:16,Low:200801}};

    SP.Ribbon.WebPartComponent.registerWithPageManager(initInfo);

    var wpcomp = SP.Ribbon.WebPartComponent.get_instance();

    var hid;

    hid = document.getElementById("_wpSelected");

    if (hid != null)

    {

        var wpid = hid.value;

        if (wpid.length > 0)

        {

            var zc = document.getElementById(wpid);

            if (zc != null)

                wpcomp.selectWebPart(zc, false);

        }

    }

    hid = document.getElementById("_wzSelected");

    if (hid != null)

    {

        var wzid = hid.value;

        if (wzid.length > 0)

        {

            wpcomp.selectWebPartZone(null, wzid);

        }

    }

};
